    var vars = [], hash;
    var q = document.URL.split('?')[1];
    if (q != undefined) {
        q = q.split('&');
        for (var i = 0; i < q.length; i++) {
            hash = q[i].split('=');
            vars.push(hash[1].replace("%20", " "));
            vars[hash[0]] = hash[1].replace("%20", " ");
        }
    }

    var timeWxViewModel = function () {
        var self = this;

        this.showFilterLists = ko.observableArray();
        this.cacheTimeUtc = new moment(new moment().utc());
        this.WxDataList = ko.observableArray();

        this.orgFilter = ko.observable();

        if (typeof wxOrg != 'undefined')
            this.orgFilter(wxOrg);

        this.orgFilters = ko.dependentObservable(function () {
            if (self.WxDataList) {
                var orgs = ko.utils.arrayMap(self.WxDataList(), function (item) { return item.org() });
                orgs.push("");
                return ko.utils.arrayGetDistinctValues(orgs).sort();
            }
        });

        this.regionFilter = ko.observable();

        if (typeof wxRegion != 'undefined')
            this.regionFilter(wxRegion);

        this.regionFilters = ko.dependentObservable(function () {
            var regions;
            if (self.filterWxLoc) {
                regions = ko.utils.arrayMap(self.filterWxLoc(), function (item) {
                    return item.region;
                });
            }
            else {
                regions = ko.utils.arrayMap(self.WxDataList(), function (item) {
                    return item.region;
                });
            }
            regions.push("");
            return ko.utils.arrayGetDistinctValues(regions).sort();
        });

        this.wxLocFilter = ko.observable();
        this.wxLocFilters = ko.dependentObservable(function () {
            var wxLocs;
            if (self.filterWxLoc) {
                wxLocs = ko.utils.arrayMap(self.filterWxLoc(), function (item) {
                    return item.city;
                });
            }
            else {
                wxLocs = ko.utils.arrayMap(self.WxDataList(), function (item) {
                    return item.city;
                });
            }
            wxLocs.push("");
            return wxLocs.sort();
        });

        this.currentWxLocId = 0;
        function getCurrentWxLoc(currentWxLocId) {
            return ko.utils.arrayFirst(ko.utils.unwrapObservable(self.WxDataList), function (wxObj) {
                return wxObj.locationId == self.currentWxLocId;
            });
        };

        this.filterWxLoc = ko.dependentObservable(function () {

            // EDS Shortcut to filter a single location.
            if (window.wxLocation) {
                var wxLocFilteredWxList = ko.utils.arrayFilter(ko.utils.unwrapObservable(self.WxDataList), function (i) {
                    return i.city == wxLocation;
                });

                if (wxLocFilteredWxList.length > 0) {
                    self.showFilterLists(false);
                    return wxLocFilteredWxList;
                }
            }

            if (window.wxRegion && !self.regionFilter())
                self.regionFilter(wxRegion);

            if (window.wxOrg && !self.orgFilter())
                self.orgFilter(wxOrg);

            var WxDataFilteredList = ko.utils.unwrapObservable(self.WxDataList);

            if (self.orgFilter()) {
                var orgFilteredWxList = ko.utils.arrayFilter(ko.utils.unwrapObservable(WxDataFilteredList), function (i) {
                    return i.org() == self.orgFilter();
                });

                if (orgFilteredWxList.length > 0)
                    WxDataFilteredList = orgFilteredWxList;
            }

            if (self.regionFilter()) {
                var regionFilteredWxList = ko.utils.arrayFilter(ko.utils.unwrapObservable(WxDataFilteredList), function (i) {
                    return i.region == self.regionFilter();
                });

                if (regionFilteredWxList.length > 0)
                    WxDataFilteredList = regionFilteredWxList;
            }

            if (self.wxLocFilter()) {
                var wxLocFilteredWxList = ko.utils.arrayFilter(ko.utils.unwrapObservable(WxDataFilteredList), function (i) {
                    return i.city == self.wxLocFilter();
                });

                if (wxLocFilteredWxList.length > 0)
                    WxDataFilteredList = wxLocFilteredWxList;
            }

            return WxDataFilteredList;
        });

        this.filtersLink = ko.dependentObservable(function () {
            var linkQueryArray = [];

            if (self.orgFilter())
                linkQueryArray.push("org=" + self.orgFilter());

            if (self.regionFilter())
                linkQueryArray.push("region=" + self.regionFilter());

            if (self.wxLocFilter())
                linkQueryArray.push("city=" + self.wxLocFilter());

            var rootUrl = document.URL.substr(0, document.URL.indexOf('?'));

            if (linkQueryArray.length > 0)
                return rootUrl + "?" + linkQueryArray.join("&");
            else
                return rootUrl;
        });

        self.Refresh = function (setFilter) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                url: "/SiteAssets/data/wx.js?rand=" + Math.random() * (50000),
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    var parsed = eval(result);
                    for (i = 0; i < parsed.WxDataList.length; i++) {
                        var wxLocVM = new wxLocViewModel(parsed.WxDataList[i]);
                        self.currentWxLocId = wxLocVM.locationId;
                        var currentMatchWxLoc = getCurrentWxLoc();

                        if (currentMatchWxLoc) {
                            self.WxDataList.replace(currentMatchWxLoc, wxLocVM);
                        }
                        else
                            self.WxDataList.push(wxLocVM);
                    }
                    self.cacheTimeUtc = parsed.cacheTimeUtc;
                    setTimeout(self.Refresh, getMillisecondsUntilNextHalfHour());

                    if (setFilter) {
                        if (vars.org)
                            self.orgFilter(vars.org);

                        if (vars.region)
                            self.regionFilter(vars.region);

                        if (vars.city)
                            self.wxLocFilter(vars.city);
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        function getMillisecondsUntilNextHalfHour() {
            var minutesTill = 60 - new Date().getMinutes();
            if (minutesTill > 30)
                minutesTill = minutesTill - 30;
            return minutesTill * 60 * 1000;
        }

        if (this.WxDataList.length === 0)
            this.Refresh(true);

    }

    function wxLocViewModel(WxData) {
        var self = this;
        self.$type = 'wxLocViewModel';
        var locationData = WxData.WxLocation;

        self.locationId = locationData.id;
        self.timeZone = locationData.timeZone;
        self.wxTime = ko.observable(new moment(WxData.wxTime).tz(self.timeZone).format('LT'));
        self.wxDate = ko.observable(new moment(WxData.wxTime).tz(self.timeZone).format('ddd'));
        self.city = locationData.city;
        self.country = locationData.country;
        self.label = locationData.city + ", " + locationData.country;
        self.program = locationData.program;

        self.region = locationData.region;
        self.type = locationData.type;
        self.org = ko.observable(locationData.org);

        self.summary = ko.observable(WxData.summary);
        self.longSummary = ko.observable(WxData.longSummary);
        self.icon = ko.observable("/SiteAssets/i/" + WxData.icon + ".svg");
        self.currentTempC = ko.observable(WxData.currentTemp.C);
        self.currentTempF = ko.observable(WxData.currentTemp.F);
        self.cloudCover = ko.observable(WxData.cloudCover);
        self.humidity = ko.observable(WxData.humidity);
        self.windSpeedKnots = ko.observable(WxData.windInfo.Knots);
        self.windDirection = ko.observable(WxData.windInfo.windDirection);
        self.lat = locationData.coord.lat;
        self.lon = locationData.coord.lon;
        self.precipIn = ko.observable(WxData.precipLast3Hrs.inches);
        self.precipCm = ko.observable(WxData.precipLast3Hrs.cm);

        self.moreInfoUrl = locationData.opWorldUrl;
        self.mapUrl = encodeURI("https://www.google.com/maps/place/" + self.label.replace("PNG", "Papua+New+Guinea"));
        self.WikiUrl = encodeURI(locationData.wikipediaUrl);
        self.MafUrl = encodeURI(locationData.mafUrl);

        var dateTime = new moment();
        if (self.timeZone === 'GMT') {
            self.localName = 'GMT';
            self.localFormattedTime = ko.observable(dateTime.utc().format('LT'));
            self.localFormattedDate = ko.observable(dateTime.utc().format('LL'));
            self.localWeekDayName = ko.observable(dateTime.utc().format('ddd'));
        } else {
            self.localName = self.timeZone.substring(self.timeZone.indexOf('/') + 1, self.timeZone.length);
            self.localFormattedTime = ko.observable(dateTime.utc().tz(self.timeZone).format('LT'));
            self.localFormattedDate = ko.observable(dateTime.utc().tz(self.timeZone).format('LL'));
            self.localWeekDayName = ko.observable(dateTime.utc().tz(self.timeZone).format('ddd'));
        }

        // If there is no label name passed, it will use the timezone name or GMT.
        if (self.label) self.localName = self.label;

        self.tick = function () {
            var dateTime = new moment();
            if (self.localName === 'GMT') {
                self.localFormattedTime(dateTime.utc().format('LT'));
                self.localFormattedDate(dateTime.utc().format('LL'));
                self.localWeekDayName(dateTime.utc().format('ddd'));
            } else {
                self.localFormattedTime(dateTime.utc().tz(self.timeZone).format('LT'));
                self.localFormattedDate(dateTime.utc().tz(self.timeZone).format('LL'));
                self.localWeekDayName(dateTime.utc().tz(self.timeZone).format('ddd'));
            }
        };
        setInterval(self.tick, 10 * 1000);
    }

    var vm = new timeWxViewModel();
    ko.applyBindings(vm);
    </script>
